We're doing this for the long haul. We think there's a real need and hunger for (more) serious reporting and analysis from a right of center view that isn't about cheap clickbait or fan-service or simply winning the next election for a team. The end. 9/9
Last, on my new venture with @stephenfhayes, I don't want to get dragged into defending it against hypotheticals and imaginary b.s. but we don't see this as being about Trump, pro or con. If anything it's more post-Trump than anti-Trump. 8/
I think the reason "Trump-skeptical" enrages so many is that it allows for two possibilities: That Trump can do wrong and that Trump can do right. That bugs both tribes of absolutists (particularly on this website). 7/
The way so many elected GOPers have responded to Trump &amp; Trumpism have helped me realize that skepticism of politicians is vital -- regardless of partisan affiliation/ideology. It's always easy to be skeptical of the other team, I've become skeptical of teams, period.  6/
But there's a broader reason why I am Trump skeptical. The last two years have shown me that I should be even more skeptical of ALL politicians. Bill Rusher, the longtime publisher of NR used to tell young'ns "politicians will always disappoint you." 5/
There's also a left cult of personality on Trump, too. They veer towards thinking he's an *evil* genius. He's not that either. That's why I never went heavy for the collusion stuff. Not b/c he isn't morally capable of it, but because he's likely managerially incapable of it 4/
I use "Trump-skeptical," in part because I think the cult of personality around Trump is so nuts. He's not a stable genius (Neither stable, nor genius). He's not a great dealmaker. He's not a good person. But he's also not Hitler (Hitler could have repealed Obamacare btw). 3/
I mean go ask MAGA Twitter whether I am onboard the Trump Train, ffs. This is the problem with being neither resistance, nor MAGA. Both have a black-and-white view. If you're not resistance, you're a Trumper. If you're not MAGA you're resistance. It's all so stupid. 2/
